<text>Update, 12/4/17:  Went this morning, got a breakfast burrito to go.  It was excellent!  If you're living or working in the Natomas area drop by and give Willie J's a try.  Good food, large portions.

I work in the area and I am always on the lookout for a good burger place.  I discovered this place today and went to give it a try.  A bit hard to find, tucked back a bit from the other businesses, but find it I did.  I ordered a double cheeseburger and a large fries.  I'm all about the fries.  I can tolerate any greasy spoon's food as long as they have good fries.  Well, I was very happy with them, they were hot and crispy and nicely seasoned (they have several varieties, but I just got 'traditional').  I should have just gone with the regular size, as the large fries filled half of the giant tray they served the food on.  For the burger I went with the bacon cheeseburger, and I asked them to make it a double.  The burger was hand formed, cooked perfectly and very juicy.  I could barely get my mouth around it!  All in all a very positive experience.  I will return.  I only gave 4 stars due to the cleanliness.  All of the tables were dirty and the trash was overflowing, but it was just after the 12 o'clock hour, so maybe they had a rush.  When I came in there was only one other customer in there eating, but a couple of others came in while I ate.  Worth a try if you like home-style burgers and fries.  Very good. Kid who took my order was very courteous and even brought my food out to me.< /text>< Pictures>

<date>1396021586954< /date><rating>3< /rating>< review>
Mini bar is just that, mini.  This small establishment it a fine place for a drink with great cocktails, jazz playing and some cool art on the walls.  There are some tables up front and a small back room and a arching bar in the middle.  If there are more than about 10 people in the bar it feels kinda crowded.  It is also a challenge to get to the restroom which is precariously places in a tight corner.  Overall though good crowd, good drinks and fun place on Divis.</review>

<username>gevorg cholakyan< /username><Date>1531714941325< /Date>< Rating>
4<//Rating>
< Review>
We really like this place for a quick bite during lunch. It's easily accessible right off the freeway. I've had the gyro wrap with rice, the chicken shawarma and their hummus. Everything is well seasoned with all the right traditional spices. You have to ask for extra garlic sauce! Their garlic dip is amazing! This is a legit Middle Eastern spot!  One of my major pet peeves is day-old pita bread. Every time I've gone into this spot I've always had fresh pita bread. It's delicious to have in a wrap or just dip in their hummus. Their chicken is never over cooked and their beef is always perfectly cooked. I do wish the place was a little bigger with more seating options. But the idea of a smaller hole in the wall ethnic restaurant is appealing to those of us who want to go in for a quick bite and experience authentic food. I'd like to see them have more drink options moving forward, more traditional Middle Eastern drinks would be fantastic with their meals. I would suggest ordering ahead of time that way when you arrive your food is ready, sometimes there could be a long wait.< /Review>

< review>
We have been big fans of Gangadin for the last ten years.  A friend of ours recommended we check them out as a candidate to cater our wedding back in 2010.  After sampling many other Indian restaurants, they won us over not only with their delicious, fresh fare but also their genuine care into making our day perfect with great service.  They were GREAT!  We have eaten there many times over this decade.  We have had gatherings with friends at their restaurant both large and small.  They never disappoint.  It's family owned and operated and they treat you like a member of their own when you dine in.  Sadly, they cannot allow diners at this time so I encourage anyone who loves Indian cuisine to try them out and/or continue ordering take out to support this great family business.  We must support our local small businesses.  It would be a sad, sad day if they had to close permanently because of this virus crisis.  We love you guys!!  (Gene and Ann Kirkland)<//review>
